< Review>
I called first, and came to the place with a $27 plus certificate coupon, also specifying "pass or free re-take". Once there, he told me that he had to charge more, because it was a van, and he had to remove the dog house. He then tested my van, which passed the computer testing (and by the way he never had to remove the dog house, as he said he would have to), and ended up failing it anyway, as per his own visual inspection the gas tank cap seal had small cracks (it was not leaking though), and a small light bulb needed to be replaced on the cluster. Of course, he told me that if desired, he had some gas plugs for sale... I went to a nearby auto parts store, baught a gas plug, a light bulb, installed all this, and returned to the testing place. There, I was charged another $25 for the "free retake...". Total cost: $65. This place is a rip off, very unprofessional, with poor basic equipment, and no respect for the customer, as I forgot to mention also, that as I first got there, I went to the counter, and the tech saw me, waved at me acknowledging that he was going to get to me, and continued talking and laughing with his friend the mechanic next door for maybe 10 minutes , while I was waiting and could see and hear them...
Last but not least, when i got home, I noticed that the under dash bracket supporting the obd2 plug was broken, and hanging. I can admit that sometimes older plastic can brake - it happens -, but what I don't accept, is that he did not mention it when he broke it, and just left it like that... so low.< /Review>

<username>GT Ford<//username>< rate>
3</rate>
<response>None<//response>< Text>
I am torn in my review of this establishment because i visit here on a semi daily basis i have a good friend who lives here and i live a mile or so away. Its a delightfully tranquil place to reside and in general i would encourage any veteran and his or her immediate family to apply for residency. My problem is that the rule structure the management maintains over the population can be somewhat draconian. Ex: my friend is in his mid 60s and not that quick on his feet i was watching movies with him.late in the day and wanted to run home for a minute to feed my dogs. He gave me his gate key so that he would not have to get up and come let me in. I ran into one of the guards who had seen me on more than one occasion before this day. He attempted to grill me in what i felt was a disrespectful fashion and then when he realized i was not going to answer his questions tried to reassure me i was not in trouble like u was a ten year old. First if all i am an accomplished human being with a masters degree and a 25 year old career of some note and he attempted  to treat me like i had stolen something. I later found out that my friend received a memo from the manager that reprimanded him for allowing me use of the key. In my time visiting there i have been made privy to little comments made and have for some time been concerned about the content of these comments. I have wondered if many of comments would have been made if i were not African American. My friend is of Irish derivation. I am a novice in dealing with housing issues of this nature but am still concerned by what i see and here. But other than that its calm quiet environment is very nice it seems safe and if not particularly friendly at least tranquil.</Text>

<Text>Back in early February of 2020, I went to my GP Doctor for my annual physical. Had a series of routine blood tests and received some very negative news. My A1C was at 9.7 and all of my Lipids were NOT good. Triglycerides were 310 and "combined" Cholesterol was 295. Plus I was at my highest weight I had ever been at in life. My GP Doctor gave me  prescriptions for Metformin and a Statin drug (which I never ended up taking - after all).

The day I heard the results I was heading to Las Vegas for a weekend with my two best friends. What a way to start a vacation in "Sin City." Lol.  I did not want to take the meds, because of the many possible side effects, so I decided to change my habits right then and there. I cut out all "white" substance from my diet - no sugar, flour, rice, or dairy. Within six weeks, I had dropped my A1C to 7.8, Triglycerides were down to 244 and combined cholesterol at 246. Not great, but moving in the right direction. Plus, I had lost 10 lbs. I was on my way.

The week before the blood test I referenced above, I had the great fortune to discover Advanced Functional Medicine (AFM). What a lifesaver, this place was! I received my program and followed it religiously! The shopping list, prescribed diet / recipes, cleanse routine, supplements, etc. If you completely embrace their program, you will be amazed at the results obtainable and achieved.

By my second blood test, my A1C was at 6.4 and triglycerides had dropped to 149 and my combined cholesterol was at 193! Holy smokes, I was feeling good. Also dropped another 15 lbs; total weight loss at that point was at 25 lbs and counting.

At the three month mark of the program and upon taking my third and last blood test, before starting two months of maintenance - my number were completely within "normal" ranges;  A1C at 5.6, triglycerides at 145 and combined cholesterol was 175. I am also at a total weight loss of 33 lbs and counting, whereby I am continuing to drop a pound or two a week on a regular basis. A great place to be - given where I was at in February!

In my interactions with AFM, I learned that I have food sensitivities to Gluten, Whey, Casein, and Soy. Those items created the inflammation that led to my insulin resistant state and the highly elevated A1C number.  They will not be in my diet, going forward and I will remain at these normal numbers, if I continue follow the program and take my supplements. Couldn't be happier.

In closing, the people at AFM are great (and a special shout out to Leslie); they saved my life, in so many ways! I just wish my medical insurance company (and GP Doctor) would embrace some of these alternative treatments / cures, and not only focus on the traditional medical / pharm models. If I had followed that route, I would now be locked into taking meds the rest of my life and that's not a good thing. No focus on finding out what was truly at issue with me (i.e. food sensitivities / inflammation problem that created an insulin resistant state), and always a complete push to just address the symptoms, but not a total cure. Too bad, I had to pay out of my own pocket, but better that then a life of meds and ending up worst off or dead. I can't thank, you all at AFM enough!</Text>< Pics>

I was curious to try Muscle Maker Grill and love the idea of healthy dishes. I was happy to find that they now deliver locally via Grub Hub. I really wanted to like it, however I was very disappointed in the food. I ordered a small smoothie; peach, pear and apricot. This was delicious, however it was it was a thin consistency, perhaps ice crystals had melted during delivery. I ordered the pasta with chicken breast and pieces of turkey meatballs. The pasta was overcooked and had absolutely no flavor, very bland. We had a burger that was equally bland and tasteless. The whole wheat bun was too soft and rather soggy. There is supposed to be some kind of sauce, but it lacked any flavor or seasoning. The burger was tough and overcooked. We tried the pasta salad. It had pickled cauliflower, broccoli, and carrots thrown together with curly pasta. Again no flavor, no effort and boring. This may be a good place for smoothies if ordered and consumed on site, however some spices and further techniques need to be applied to the other dishes.</text>

Tucked away in the corner of the plaza just steps away from Yogurtland. Came here for lunch with a coworker and it was my first time here! Ordered the Godfather as suggested and it was literally a giant chicken breast cooked with balsamic vinegar and served over steamed broccoli.

< Review>
Do yourself a favor, reserve a storage unit HERE!

Not only does it include amazing customer service by friendly, professional staff but it's also an affordable price for LA in a navigable location. Don't forget the convenience of managing your account online while having a flexible month to month contract :)

Obviously everyone knows that moving is stressful. My move was especially stressful, not because the fact I was moving from San Diego, but everything that you think could and couldn't go wrong...went wrong. From broken boxes from accident prone movers and sitting in traffic with empty gas tanks to wrong keys by missing landlords and ruined newly bought furniture and mishandled sentimental belongings- I begged the day to be over and naturally I dreaded my last stop:storage. It was heaven- the exact opposite of how my day was going.
Seriously I'm considering to believe in angels because when I went there, I easily spotted and found parking right away. I was greeted sincerely and helped right away! They worked with the movers and everything was stored and moved unbelievably smoothly! Words cannot express my gratitude and satisfaction. Thank you so much Stanley and Yesenia, I highly recommend you to go to this Public Storage unit!!</Review>
